        int n;
        cin >> n;
                string s;
        cin >> s;
                int p[n + 1] = {0};
        int j = 1;
        for(char c : s){
            p[j] = p[j - 1] + (int)(c - '0');
            ++j;
        }
                map<int, int> f;
        f.insert({0, 1});
                long long count = 0LL;
        for(int i = 1; i<=n; ++i){
            count = count + f[p[i] - i]*1LL;
            ++f[p[i] - i];
        }
                cout << count << endl;
    }
    return 0;

 int main(){
    int t;
    cin >> t;
    while(t--){
        vector<int> patches;
        string s;
        cin >> s;
                int cnt = 0;
        for(auto c: s){
            if(c == '0'){
                if(cnt != 0)
                    patches.push_back(cnt);
                cnt = 0;
            }
            else ++cnt;
        }
        if(cnt != 0)
            patches.push_back(cnt);
                sort(patches.begin(), patches.end(), greater<int>());
                int ans = 0;
        for(int i = 0; i<patches.size(); i+=2)
            ans+=patches[i];
        cout << ans << endl;
    }
    return 0;

 ll power(ll x, ll y, ll p = MOD){  
    ll res = 1LL; 
    x = x % p;
    if (x == 0) return 0;
    while (y > 0){
        if (y & 1LL)  
            res = (res*x) % p;
        y = y>>1LL; 
        x = (x*x) % p;  
    }  
    return res;  
}

 ll number(ll w[], int n, int s){
    int st = 0, en = n - 1, cnt = 0;
    while(st < en){
        int total = w[st] + w[en];
        if(total < s)
            ++st;
        else if(total > s)
            --en;   
        else{
            ++cnt;
            ++st;
            --en;
        }
    }
    return cnt;
}
 int main(){
 IO
 int t;
 cin >> t;
 while(t--){
  int n;
  cin >> n;
         string s;
        cin >> s;
         int ans[n] = {0};
        vi end0, end1;
        int cnt = 1;
        for(int i = 0; i<n; ++i){
            if(s[i] == '1'){
                if(end0.size()){
                    ans[i] = end0.back();
                    end0.pop_back();
                    end1.push_back(ans[i]);
                }
                else{
                    ans[i] = cnt;
                    end1.push_back(cnt++);
                }
            }
            else{
                if(end1.size()){
                    ans[i] = end1.back();
                    end1.pop_back();
                    end0.push_back(ans[i]);
                }
                else{
                    ans[i] = cnt;
                    end0.push_back(cnt++);
                }
            }
        }
         cout << cnt - 1 << endl;
        pvec(ans); cout << endl;
  }
 return 0;

 int main(){
 IO
 int t;
 cin >> t;
 while(t--){
  int n;
  cin >> n;
         ll a[n], b[n];
        ll mna = INF, mnb = INF;
        rep(i, 0, n) {
            cin >> a[i];
            mna = min(mna, a[i]);
        }
        rep(i, 0, n) {
            cin >> b[i];
            mnb = min(mnb, b[i]);
        }
         ll ans = 0;
        for(int i = 0; i<n; ++i){
            ll reqa = a[i] - mna;
            ll reqb = b[i] - mnb;
            ans+=(min(reqb, reqa) + abs(reqa - reqb));
        }
         cout << ans << endl;
 }
 return 0;

 bool *p;
vi primes;
void sieve(int n){
 p = new bool[n + 5];
 for(int i = 0; i<n + 5; ++i)
  p[i] = true;
 p[0] = p[1] = false;
 for(int i = 2; i*i <= n; ++i){
  if(p[i])
   for(int j = 2*i; j<=n; j+=i)
    p[j] = false;
 }
  primes.pb(2);
 for(int i = 3; i<=n; i+=2)
  if(p[i])
   primes.pb(i);
}
 bool dfs(vector<vi> &adj, int N, int M, int u, vi &visited, int p[], int h[]){
 visited[u] = 1;
 for(int v: adj[u]){
  if(!visited[v]){
   if((p[v] + h[v])%2 || (p[v] - h[v])%2) {
    // debug(v, N, M, p[v], h[v], h[u]);
    return false;
   }
    int happy = (p[v] + h[v])/2;
   int sad = (p[v] - h[v])/2;
    if(happy < 0 || sad < 0)
    return false;
      if(sad > M)
    N = N - happy - (sad - M);
   else 
    N-=happy;
    M = max(0, M - sad);
    if(N < 0) {
    return false;
   }
      if(!dfs(adj, happy, sad, v, visited, p, h)){
    return false;
   }
  }
 }
  visited[u] = 2;
 return true;
}
 int dfs1(vector<vi> &adj, int u, vi &visited, int p[]){
 visited[u] = 1;
 for(int v: adj[u]){
  if(!visited[v]){
   p[u]+=dfs1(adj, v, visited, p);
  }
 }
 return p[u];
}
 int main(){
 IO
 int t;
 cin >> t;
 while(t--){
  int n, m;
  cin >> n >> m;
   int p[n], h[n];
  rep(i, 0, n)
   cin >> p[i];
  rep(i, 0, n)
   cin >> h[i];
   vector<vector<int>> adj(n);
  int u, v;
  for(int i = 0; i<n - 1; ++i){
   cin >> u >> v;
   --u; --v;
   adj[u].pb(v);
   adj[v].pb(u);
  }
   vi visited(n + 1, 0);
    if((m - h[0])%2 || (m + h[0])%2){
   cout << "NO\n";
   continue;
  }
    dfs1(adj, 0, visited, p);
   for(int i = 0; i<n; ++i)
   visited[i] = 0;
   int happy = (m + h[0])/2;
  int sad = (m - h[0])/2;
   if(happy < 0 || sad < 0 || happy + sad > m){
   cout << "NO\n";
   continue;
  }
   bool res = dfs(adj, happy, sad, 0, visited, p, h);
  res ? cout << "YES\n" : cout << "NO\n";
 }
 return 0;

  int main(){
 IO
 sieve(500);
 int t;
 cin >> t;
 while(t--){
  int n;
  cin >> n;
   vi ans;
  for(int i = 0; i<n; ++i){
   ans.pb(9);
  }
  int left = (int)ceil(n*1.0/4);
  for(int i = n - 1; i>=0 && left; --i){
   ans[i] = 8;
   --left;
  }
  // pvec(ans);cout << endl;
  for(int x: ans)
   cout << x;
  cout << endl;
 }
 return 0;

  int n;

   if(n == 36){
   cout << "YES\n" << "5 6 10 15\n";
  }
  else if(n == 40){
   cout << "YES\n" << "5 6 14 15\n";
  }
  else if(n == 44){
   cout << "YES\n" << "6 7 10 21\n";
  }
  else if(n > 30){
   cout << "YES\n" << 6 << " " << 10 << " " << 14 << " " << n - 30 << endl;
  } else {
   cout << "NO\n";
  }
 }

 ll power(ll x, ll y, ll p = MOD){  
    ll res = 1LL; 
    x = x % p;
    if (x == 0) return 0;
    while (y > 0){
        if (y & 1LL)  
            res = (res*x) % p;
        y = y>>1LL; 
        x = (x*x) % p;  
    }  
    return res;  
}  
 void op(string &a, int idx){
 for(int i = 0; i<=idx;++i){
  if(a[i] == '1') a[i] = '0';
  else a[i] = '1';
 }
 reverse(a.begin(), a.begin() + idx + 1);
}
 int main(){
 IO
 int t;
 cin >> t;
  while(t--){
  int n;
  cin >> n;
   string a, b;
  cin >> a;
  cin >> b; 
   vector<int> ans;
  int bp = n - 1;
  while(bp >= 0 && a[bp] == b[bp]){
   --bp;
  }
   while(bp >= 0){
      if(a[0] != b[bp]){
    ans.pb(bp + 1);
    op(a, bp);
    --bp;
   }
   else {
    ans.pb(1);
    op(a, 0);
   }
   // cout << a << endl;
  }
   // if(a == b){
  //  cout << "DONE";
  // }
  // else 
  //  cout << "NO";
  cout << ans.size() << " ";
  pvec(ans); cout << endl;
 }
 return 0;
}#include<bits/stdc++.h>

 int main(){
 IO
 int t;
 cin >> t;
 while(t--){
  int n;
  cin >> n;
   ll arr[n];
  for(int i = 0; i<n; ++i)
   cin >> arr[i];
    int ans[n] = {0};
  ans[n-1] = 1;
   for(int i = n - 2; i>=0; --i){
   if(ans[i + 1] == 1 ){
    if(arr[i] > 1)
     ans[i] = 1;
    else
     ans[i] = 0;
   }
   else {
    ans[i] = 1;
   }
  }
   // rep(i, 0, n)
  //  cout << ans[i] << " ";
  // cout << endl;
  if(ans[0] == 1)
   cout << "First\n";
  else
   cout << "Second\n";
  }
 return 0;

 int main(){
 IO
 int t;
 cin >> t;
 while(t--){
  int n, m;
  cin >> n >> m;
   int a[n], b[m];
  int freq[1005] = {0};
  rep(i, 0, n) {
   cin >> a[i];
   ++freq[a[i]];
  }
  int ans = -1;
  rep(i, 0, m){
   cin >> b[i];
   if(freq[b[i]]){
    ans = b[i];
   }
  }
  if(ans == -1){
   cout << "NO\n";
  }
  else 
   cout << "YES\n1 " << ans << endl; 
  }
 return 0;
}#include<bits/stdc++.h>
using namespace std;
 int main(){
    int T;
    cin >> T;
    while(T--){
        string t;
        cin >> t;
                int r = 0, p = 0, s = 0;
        for(auto c : t){
            if(c == 'R') ++r;
            else if(c == 'P') ++p;
            else ++s;
        }
         char choice;
        if(r >=p && r >= s)
            choice = 'P';
        else if(p >= r && p>= s)
            choice = 'S';
        else 
            choice = 'R';
         for(int i = 0; i<(int)t.size(); ++i)
            cout << choice;
        cout << endl;
    }
    return 0;
}#include<bits/stdc++.h>
using namespace std;
 int main(){
    int t;
    cin >> t;
    while(t--){
        int n;
        cin >> n;
                int arr[n];
        for(int i = 0; i <n; ++i)
            cin >> arr[i];
                int found = -1;
        for(int i = 1; i < n - 1; ++i){
            if(arr[i] > arr[i-1] && arr[i] > arr[i + 1]){
                found = i; 
            }
        }
                found == -1 ? cout << "NO\n" : cout << "YES\n" << found << " " << found + 1 << " " << found + 2 << "\n";
    }
    return 0;

 int main(){
 IO
 int t;
 cin >> t;
 while(t--){
  int n;
  cin >> n;
   ll arr[n], count = 0;
  rep(i, 0, n){
   cin >> arr[i];
   if(arr[i] == i + 1)
    ++count;
  }
   int i = 0;
  while(i < n && arr[i] == i + 1){
   --count;
   ++i;
  }
  i = n - 1;
  while(i >= 0 && arr[i] == i + 1){
   --count;
   --i;
  }
     if(is_sorted(arr, arr + n)){
   cout << 0 << endl;
  }
  else if(count == 0)
   cout << 1 << endl;
  else
   cout << 2 << endl;
 }
 return 0;
}#include<bits/stdc++.h>
using namespace std;
 typedef long long int ll;
 int main() {
 int t;
 cin >> t;
 while(t--){
  ll n;
  cin >> n;
   vector<int> factors;
  for(ll i = 1; i*i <= n; ++i){
   if(n%i == 0)
    factors.push_back(i);
   if(n/i != i)
    factors.push_back(n/i);
  }
   ll mn = 1000000000LL, aa = 1, ab = n;
  for(int fact: factors){
   if(fact == n) continue;
   ll a = fact, b = n - fact;
   ll lcm = a*b/(__gcd(a, b));
   if(mn > lcm){
    mn = lcm;
    aa = a;
    ab = b;
   }
  }
   cout << aa << " " << ab << endl;
 }
 return 0;
}#include<bits/stdc++.h>

        cout << 3 << endl;
    }
    return 0;

 int main(){
 IO
 int t;
 cin >> t;
 while(t--){
  ll n, k;
        cin >> n >> k;
         vll arr(n);
        rep(i, 0, n)
            cin >> arr[i];
         map<int, int> res;
        for(int e: arr){
            res[(ll)ceil(e*1.0/k)*k - e] += 1;
        }
         vll ans;
        for(auto e: res){
            if(e.first > 0){
                for(int i = 0; i<e.second; ++i){
                    ans.pb(e.first + i*k);
                }
            }
        }
                if(ans.size() == 0){
            cout << 0 << endl;
            continue;
        }
        sort(all(ans));
         ll sol = 0, x = 0;
        for(int i = 0; i<ans.size(); ++i){
            if(ans[i] == x){
                ++sol;
                ++x;
            }
            else{
                sol+=(ans[i] - x + 1);
                x = ans[i] + 1;
            }
        }
         cout << sol << endl;
 }
 return 0;
}#include<bits/stdc++.h>

 int main(){
 IO
 int t;
 cin >> t;
 while(t--){
  ll n;
        cin >> n;
         string s;
        cin >> s;
         int cnt = 0, num = 0;
        for(int i = 0; i<n;++i){
            if(s[i] == '(')
                ++cnt;
            else
                --cnt;
             if(cnt < 0){
                ++num;
                cnt = 0;
            }
        }
         cout << num << endl;
 }
 return 0;

 int main(){
 IO
 int t;
 cin >> t;
 while(t--){
  ll n;
        cin >> n;
         ll tmp = n;
        if(n == 1){
            cout << 0 << endl;
            continue;
        }
         ll two = 0, three = 0;
        while(n%2 == 0){
            n/=2;
            ++two;
        }
        while(n%3 == 0){
            n/=3;
            ++three;
        }
         ll tmp2 = three;
        while(three > two){
            tmp*=2;
            --three;
        }
         while(tmp%6 == 0)
            tmp/=6;
                three = tmp2;
        if(tmp > 1){
            cout << -1 << endl;
        }
        else{
            cout << min(two, three) + 2*abs(two - three) << endl;
        }
 }
 return 0;
}#include<bits/stdc++.h>

 IO

  cin >> x >> y >> n;
         ll ans = n/x*x + y;
        if(ans > n)
            ans-=x;

 }

 ll kadane(vector<ll> a){
 int n = (int)a.size();
 ll curr = 0, mx = -1;
 for(int i = 0; i<n; ++i){
  curr+=a[i];
  mx = max(curr, mx);
  if(curr < 0)
   curr = 0;
 }
 return mx;
}
 int main(){
 IO
 int t;
 cin >> t;
 while(t--){
  int n;
  cin >> n;
  vector<ll> arr(n), c1, c2;
  for(int i = 0; i<n; ++i)
   cin >> arr[i];
  ll sum = 0;
  for(int i = 0; i<n; i+=2)
   sum+=arr[i];
   ll cc1, cc2 = -INF;
  for(int i = 1; i<n; i+=2)
   c1.push_back(arr[i] - arr[i-1]);
   cc1 = kadane(c1);
  if(n >= 3){
   for(int i = 2; i<n; i+=2)
    c2.push_back(arr[i-1] - arr[i]);
   cc2 = kadane(c2);
  }
   cout << sum + max({cc1, cc2, 0LL}) << endl;
 }
 return 0;
}#include<bits/stdc++.h>

 int main(){
 IO
 int t;
 cin >> t;
 while(t--){
  string s;
  cin >> s;
   int ones = 0, zeroes = 0;
  for(char c: s){
   if(c == '1')
    ++ones;
   else
    ++zeroes;
  }
   int res = min(zeroes, ones);
  if(res&1)
   cout << "DA\n";
  else
   cout << "NET\n";
 }
 return 0;
}#include<bits/stdc++.h>

 int main(){
 IO
 int t;
 cin >> t;
 while(t--){
  ll a, b, c, ans1, ans2;
  cin >> a >> b >> c;
  double per = c*1.0/b;
  if(per < a){
   ans2 = b;
   if(a < c)
    ans1 = 1;
   else
    ans1 = -1;
  }
  else if(per > a){
   ans1 = 1;
   ans2 = -1;
  }
  else{
   ans2 = -1;
   if(a < c)
    ans1 = 1;
   else
    ans1 = -1;
  }
   cout << ans1 << " " << ans2 << endl;
 }
 return 0;
}#include<bits/stdc++.h>
using namespace std;
 typedef long long int ll;
typedef vector<int> vi;
typedef set<int> si;
typedef set<ll> sll;

 void debug_out() { cerr << endl; }

 ll power(ll x, ll y, ll p = MOD){  
    ll res = 1LL; 
    x = x % p;
    if (x == 0) return 0;
    while (y > 0){
        if (y & 1LL)  
            res = (res*x) % p;
        y = y>>1LL; 
        x = (x*x) % p;  
    }  
    return res;  
}  
 vi primes;
void sieve(int n){
 bool p[n + 5];
 rep(i, 0, n + 5) p[i] = true;
  p[0] = p[1] = false;
 for(int i = 2; i*i<=n; ++i){
  if(p[i])
   for(int j = 2*i; j<=n; j+=i)
    p[j] = false;
 }
  for(int i = 2; i<=n; ++i)
  if(p[i])
   primes.pb(i);
}
 int main(){
 sieve(100000);
 IO
 int t;
 cin >> t;
 while(t--){
  int n, val;
  cin >> n;
  if(n == 1){
   cout << "FastestFinger\n";
  }
  else if(n == 2){
   cout << "Ashishgup\n";
  }
  else if(n%2){
   cout << "Ashishgup\n";
  }
  else{
   if((n&(n - 1)) == 0)
    cout << "FastestFinger\n";
   else{
    int two = 0;
    int tmp = n;
    while(n%2==0){
     n/=2;
     ++two;
    }
    n = tmp;
    if(two > 1){
     cout << "Ashishgup\n";
    }
    else{
     int cnt = 0;
     for(int prime: primes){
      if(prime > n)
       break;
      while(n%prime == 0){
       n/=prime;
       if(prime%2)
        ++cnt;
      }
      if(cnt > 1)
       break;
     }
     if(n!=1)
      ++cnt;
          if(cnt == 1)
      cout << "FastestFinger\n";
     else
      cout << "Ashishgup\n";
    }
   }
  }
 }
 return 0;
}#include<bits/stdc++.h>

 rep(i, 0, 10)

   curr*=cnt[i];

  }
 }

 int *factors;
 void getFactors(){
 for(int i = 0; i<10000005; ++i) factors[i] = i;
  for(int i = 2; i*i<= 10000005; ++i){
  if(factors[i] == i){
   for(int j = 2*i; j<= 10000005; j+=i)
    factors[j] = min(factors[j], i);
  }
 }
}
 int main(){
 IO
 factors = new int[10000005];
 getFactors();
  int n;
 cin >> n;
 int arr[n];
  rep(i, 0, n)
  cin >> arr[i];
  int ans1[n + 1], ans2[n + 1];
 memset(ans1, -1, sizeof(ans1));
 memset(ans2, -1, sizeof(ans2));
 int curr;
 rep(i, 0, n){
  vector<int> fact;
  int d1, d2;
  curr = arr[i];
  while(curr!=1){
   fact.push_back(factors[curr]);
   while(curr%(fact.back()) == 0) 
    curr/=(fact.back());
  }
   if(fact.size() <= 1)
   continue; 
  // pvec(fact); cout << endl;
  d1 = fact[0];
  d2 = 1;
  for(int i = 1; i<fact.size(); ++i)
   d2*=fact[i];
   // debug(d1, d2);
  ans1[i] = d1;
  ans2[i] = d2;
 }
  for(int i = 0; i<n; ++i)
  cout << ans1[i] << " ";
 cout << endl;
 for(int i = 0; i<n; ++i)
  cout << ans2[i] << " ";
 return 0;

 int dfs(vector<vi> adj, int u, vi &visited, vi &nodes){
    visited[u] = 1;
    for(auto v: adj[u]){
        if(!visited[v]){
            nodes[u]+=1 + dfs(adj, v, visited, nodes);
        }
    }
    visited[u] = 2;
    return nodes[u];
}
 int main(){
    IO
    int t;
    cin >> t;
    while(t--){
        int n, x;
        cin >> n >> x;
         vector<vi> adj(n);
        int u, v;
        rep(i, 0, n - 1){
            cin >> u >> v;
            --u; --v;
            adj[u].pb(v);
            adj[v].pb(u);
        }
         if((int)adj[x - 1].size() <= 1){
            cout << "Ayush\n";
            continue;
        }
        // cout << "hi" << endl;
        vi nodes(n, 0), visited(n, 0);
        dfs(adj, x - 1, visited, nodes);
         int sum = 0;
        for(auto children: adj[x - 1]) {
            sum+=nodes[children];
            // cout << children + 1 << " " << nodes[children] << endl;
        }
        sum+=(int)adj[x - 1].size() - 1;
        if(sum&1) cout << "Ashish\n";
        else cout << "Ayush\n";
    }   
    return 0;

 int main(){
    IO
    int t;
    cin >> t;
    while(t--){
        string s, tmp;
        cin >> s;
                int n = (int)s.size();
        int pref1[n + 1] = {0}, pref0[n + 1] = {0}, suff1[n + 1] = {0}, suff0[n + 1] = {0};
         rep(i, 0, n){
            if(s[i] == '1') {
                pref1[i + 1] = pref1[i] + 1;
                pref0[i + 1] = pref0[i];
            }
            else {
                pref1[i + 1] = pref1[i];
                pref0[i + 1] = pref0[i] + 1;
            }
        }
        for(int i = n - 1; i>=0; --i){
            if(s[i] == '1') {
                suff1[i] = suff1[i + 1] + 1;
                suff0[i] = suff0[i + 1];
            }
            else {
                suff1[i] = suff1[i + 1];
                suff0[i] = suff0[i + 1] + 1;
            }
        }
         int mn = INF;
        rep(i, 0, n + 1)
            mn = min(mn, pref0[i] + suff1[i]);
         rep(i, 0, n + 1)
            mn = min(mn, pref1[i] + suff0[i]);
         cout << mn << endl;
    }   
    return 0;

 int main(){
 IO
    int t;
    cin >> t;
    while(t--){
        int n;
        cin >> n;
        vi arr(n);
        rep(i, 0, n) cin >> arr[i];
                sort(all(arr));
         int pres = 1, i = 0;
        while(i < n){
            if(pres >= arr[i]){
                ++pres;
                ++i;
                continue;
            }
             int cnt = 0;
            while(i< n && pres + cnt < arr[i]){
                ++cnt;
                ++i;
             }
            if(i == n) break; 
            else pres+=cnt;
        }
         cout << pres << endl;
    }
 return 0;
}#include<bits/stdc++.h>

 ll power(ll x, ll y, ll p = MOD){  
    ll res = 1LL; 
    x = x % p;
    if (x == 0) return 0;
    while (y > 0){
        if (y & 1LL)  
            res = (res*x) % p;
        y = y>>1LL; 
        x = (x*x) % p;  
    }  
    return res;  
}  
 int main(){
 IO
    int t;
    cin >> t;
    while(t--){
        int n, m;
        cin >> n >> m;
        if(n == 1 && m == 1) {
            cout << 1 << endl;
            continue;
        }
        else if(n == 1 || m == 1){
            cout << ceil(max(n, m)/2.0) << endl;
            continue;
        }
         int div = max(n, m), mul = min(n, m), ans;
        if(div&1) ans = mul*(div - 1)/2 + (int)ceil(mul/2.0);
        else ans = mul*div/2;
         // swap(div, mul);
        // if(div&1) ans = min(ans, mul*(div - 1)/2 + (int)ceil(mul/2.0));
        // else ans = min(ans, mul*div/2);
                cout << ans << endl;
    }
 return 0;

 int dist(string a, string b){
    int n = a.size();
    int diff = 0;
    rep(i, 0, n){   
        if(a[i]!=b[i]) ++diff;
    }
    return diff;
}
 int main(){
 IO
 int t;
 cin >> t;
 while(t--){
  ll n, m;
        cin >> n >> m;
        vector<string> grid(n);
        rep(i, 0, n){
            cin >> grid[i];
        }
                set<string> al;
        rep(i, 0, n){
            rep(j, 0, m){
                char c = grid[i][j];
                rep(k, 0, 26){
                    grid[i][j] = 'a' + k;
                    if(grid[i][j]!=c) al.insert(grid[i]);
                }
                grid[i][j] = c;
            }
        }
        // cout << "-------" << endl;
        // for(auto e: grid)cout << e << endl;
        string ans = "";
        for(auto ty: al){
            int cnt = 0;
            rep(i, 0, n){
                 if(dist(ty, grid[i]) >= 2){
                    break;
                }
                else ++cnt;
            }
            if(cnt == n){
                ans = ty;
                break;
            }
        }
         ans == "" ? cout << -1 << endl : cout << ans << endl;
 }      
 return 0;
}#include<bits/stdc++.h>

 int main(){
 IO
 int t;
 cin >> t;
 while(t--){
  ll n;
        cin >> n;
        vector<string> grid(n);
        rep(i, 0, n){
            cin >> grid[i];
        }
        bool f = true;
        for(int i = 0; i<n - 1 && f; ++i){
            for(int j = 0; j<n - 1; ++j){
                if(grid[i][j] == '1'){
                    if(!(grid[i + 1][j] == '1' || grid[i][j+1] == '1')){
                        f = false;
                        break;
                    }
                }
            }
        }
         f ? cout << "YES\n" : cout << "NO\n";
 }  
 return 0;
}#include<bits/stdc++.h>

 int main(){
 IO
 int t;
 cin >> t;
 while(t--){
  ll n, k;
        cin >> n >> k;
        if(k >=n ){
            cout << 1 << endl;
            continue;
        }
         ll mn = INF;
        for(ll i = 1; i*i<=n; ++i){
            if(n%i == 0){
                if(i <=k) mn = min(mn, n/i);
                if(n/i <= k) mn = min(mn, i);
            }
        }
         cout << mn << endl; 
 }  
 return 0;
}
